<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блоко</a> (2485)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ablъko</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂ébōl</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂ébl̥</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блоко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jábloko</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блока</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блоки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>apple
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ада́мово <a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блоко</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">adámovo jábloko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Adam's apple</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блоко</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздор.html>раздо́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jábloko</b> razdóra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">apple of discord</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блоках</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v jáblokax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dappled (<i>usually of a horse</i>)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>eyeball <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глазной.html>глазно́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блоко</a></span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*abolnь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂ebol-ni-</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яблоня.html>я́блоня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jáblonja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яблоня.html>я́блони</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яблоня.html>я́блони</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яблоня.html>я́блонь</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:яблочник.html>я́блочник</a> (30350)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блоко</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jábloko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яблочник.html>я́блочник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jábločnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яблочник.html>я́блочника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яблочник.html>я́блочники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яблочник.html>я́блочников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> apple grower or seller</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> member of an organization or political party using an apple as a symbol</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> insect that feeds exclusively on apples</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neologism<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> avid user of Apple computers</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking<span class="ib-comma">,</span> inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> casserole or cake containing apples</li></ol>

***явить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:явить.html>яви́ть</a> (14234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ꙗвити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">javiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*aviti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явить.html>яви́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">javítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:являть.html>явля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to show <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to have somebody see something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:явиться.html>яви́ться</a> (1218)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явить.html>яви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">javítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явиться.html>яви́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">javítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:являться.html>явля́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to report (in person), to appear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:явиться.html>яви́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Javísʹ</b> ko mne.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Come to me.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to turn up</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явить.html>яви́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">javítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:явка.html>я́вка</a> (14447)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явить.html>яви́ть</a>(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">javítʹ(sja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явка.html>я́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jávka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явка.html>я́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явка.html>я́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явка.html>я́вок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>presence, attendance</li>
<li>secret address</li>
<li>turnout</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:являться.html>явля́ться</a> (406)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:являть.html>явля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">javljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:являться.html>явля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">javljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явиться.html>яви́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to report (in person), to appear</li>
<li>to turn up</li>
<li>to be (+ instrumental case, <i>only imperfective</i>)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явный.html>я́вный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jávnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:явственно.html>я́вственно</a> (7494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явственный.html>я́вственный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jávstvennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явственно.html>я́вственно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jávstvenno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-я́вственно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)я́вственнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-я́вственно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)я́вственней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>clearly, distinctly, perceptibly</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явственно.html>я́вственно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jávstvenno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явственный.html>я́вственный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jávstvennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">я́вств(<a href = vnd.unilang:замедлить.html>енный</a>)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jávstv(ennyj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явь.html>явь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">javʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ствовать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явствовать.html>я́вствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jávstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be obvious, to be clear</li></ol>

***явь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:явь.html>явь</a> (15788)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*avь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">obvious, apparent, real</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂ew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">apparent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">jawa</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">я́ва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jáva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">ява́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">javá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">яв</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jav</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явь.html>явь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">javʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явить.html>я́ви</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явить.html>я́ви</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явь.html>я́вей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reality</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ягель.html>я́гель</a> (27802)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sami_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Sami languages">Sami</a></span> language descended from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Samic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Samic">Proto-Samic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="smi-pro">*jeakēl</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ягель.html>я́гель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jágelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ягель.html>я́геля</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ягода.html>я́года</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jágoda</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">berry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ица</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, because of the round shape of buttocks: compare the dialectal senses.

***ягодка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ягодка.html>я́годка</a> (20594)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ядъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jadŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <span class="Cyrs" lang="orv">ѣдъ</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="tr Latn">ědŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jadъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яд.html>яд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jad</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яд.html>я́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яд.html>я́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яд.html>я́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>poison, venom
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1999</b>,  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сойти.html>сошла́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ума́</a></span>”, performed by t.A.T.u.:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:медленный.html>ме́дленный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:яд.html>яд</a></b><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>сводит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ума́</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говоря́т</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:виноватый.html>винова́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сама́</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto médlennyj <b>jad</b><br />Éto svodit s umá<br />A oní govorját - vinováta samá</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It's slow poison<br />It's making me crazy<br />And they say it's all my fault</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> something or someone that has a harmful effect on someone</li></ol>

***ядерный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ядерный.html>я́дерный</a> (5432)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ядро.html>ядро́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jadró</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ядреный.html>ядрёный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jadrjónyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ядерный.html>я́дерный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jádernyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>nuclear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ядерный.html>я́дерное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сырье.html>сырьё</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jádernoje</b> syrʹjó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nuclear raw material</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ядро.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ядро.html>ядро́</a> (6234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ędro</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ядро.html>ядро́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jadró</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ядро.html>ядра́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ядро.html>я́дра</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ядро.html>я́дер</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> seed, stone</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cannonball, round shot</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> cytology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nucleus</li>
<li>nucleus (cluster of nucleons)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">astronomy<span class="ib-comma">,</span> geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> core <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a planet, star, or galaxy</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">astronomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nucleus <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a comet</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> core <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a processor</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> kernel <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of an operating system</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cone <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a flame</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">athletics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shot <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">heavy iron ball</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sociology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> core members, activists <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in a group</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> core <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">set of allocations that cannot be improved</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> kernel <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">set of all elements mapped to the zero element by a transformation</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***язва.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:язва.html>я́зва</a> (5213)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ꙗзва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jazva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jazva</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Prussian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Prussian language">Old Prussian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="prg">eyswo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wound</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">áiža</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crack, rift</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">aĩza</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chasm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:язва.html>я́зва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jázva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:язва.html>я́звы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:язва.html>я́звы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:язва.html>я́зв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ulcer, sore
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:язва.html>я́зва</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:желудок.html>желу́дка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jázva</b> želúdka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stomach/gastric ulcer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:язва.html>я́зва</a></b> двенадцатиперстной <a href = vnd.unilang:кишка.html>кишки́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jázva</b> dvenadcatiperstnoj kiškí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">duodenal ulcer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">моровая <b><a href = vnd.unilang:язва.html>я́зва</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">morovaja <b>jázva</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">plague</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сибирский.html>сиби́рская</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язва.html>я́зва</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sibírskaja jázva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">anthrax</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>sore, evil</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pest, viper <i>(malicious person)</i></li></ol>

***язвить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:язвить.html>язви́ть</a> (17980)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:язвить.html>язви́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jazvítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:съязвить.html>съязви́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bite, to sting, to wound</li>
<li>to taunt, to mock</li></ol>
